<li id="cite_note-Steven_Schoenherr-389"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Steven_Schoenherr_389-0"><sup><b>381.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Steven_Schoenherr_389-1"><sup><b>381.1</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Steven Schoenherr. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20080509054959/http://history.sandiego.edu/gen/WW2Timeline/espionage.html" rel="nofollow">Code Breaking in World War II</a>. <a href="/wiki/%E8%81%96%E5%9C%B0%E7%89%99%E5%93%A5%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8" title="圣地牙哥大学">圣地牙哥大学</a>（University of San Diego）. 2007年 [2012年4月21日查阅] <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#54595d; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英文）</span>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-390"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-390">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Neil C. Rowe和Hy Rothstein. <a class="external text" href="http://www.au.af.mil/au/awc/awcgate/nps/mildec.htm" rel="nofollow">Deception for Defense of Information Systems: Analogies from Conventional Warfare</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20101123031630/http://www.au.af.mil/au/awc/awcgate/nps/mildec.htm" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%9C%8B%E6%B5%B7%E8%BB%8D%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="美国海军研究所">美国海军研究所</a>（Naval Postgraduate School）. 2007年 [2012年4月21日查阅] <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#54595d; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英文）</span>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-391"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-391">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.idsia.ch/~juergen/zuse.html" rel="nofollow">KONRAD ZUSE (1910-1995)</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20100324122611/http://www.idsia.ch/~juergen/zuse.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）. <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=IDSIA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="IDSIA（页面不存在）">IDSIA</a> [2012年4月21日查阅] <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#54595d; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英文）</span>. "Konrad Zuse builds Z1, world's first program-controlled computer. Despite certain mechanical engineering problems it had all the basic ingredients of modern machines, using the binary system and today's standard separation of storage and control. Zuse's 1936 patent application (Z23139/GMD Nr. 005/021) also suggests a von Neumann architecture (re-invented in 1945) with program and data modifiable in storage."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-392"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-392">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a class="external text" href="https://www.acs.org/content/acs/en/education/whatischemistry/landmarks/flemingpenicillin.html" rel="nofollow">Alexander Fleming Discovery and Development of Penicillin - Landmark</a>. American Chemical Society.  <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2022-10-09</span>]</span> <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英语）</span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E5%A4%A7%E6%88%98&amp;rft.atitle=Alexander+Fleming+Discovery+and+Development+of+Penicillin+-+Landmark&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=American+Chemical+Society&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.acs.org%2Fcontent%2Facs%2Fen%2Feducation%2Fwhatischemistry%2Flandmarks%2Fflemingpenicillin.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
</ol></div>

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.80.A3.E7.B5.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部连结">外部连结</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E5%A4%A7%E6%88%98&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：外部连结">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
